    				v5:warn("weapon does not have a receiver")
    				v62:equip(p1.weapons.equipped)
    			send_bindable_message(v8, {
    			})
    			v62:equip(p1.weapon_id)
    				send_bindable_message(v8, {
    				})
    			v62:unequip()
    			v62:destroy_weapons()
    			v62:remove_weapon(p1.weapon_id)
    	end))
    	v32:GiveTask(v7:Connect(function(p1, p2) --[[ Line: 123 | Upvalues: data (copy) ]]
    				data.char_details[3] = p2.team
    	end))
    	v32:GiveTask(replication.OnClientEvent:ConnectParallel(function(p1, p2) --[[ Line: 132 | Upvalues: ingame_id (copy), BitBuffer (ref), NetworkEncode (ref), unpack_number16 (ref), t2 (copy), t (copy), v2 (ref), send_bindable_message (ref), v8 (ref) ]]
    			local v1 = BitBuffer.new(64)
    			v1:import(p2)
    			local v22 = NetworkEncode.read_time(v1)
    			local v3 = unpack_number16(v1:read_u16())
    			local v4 = v3[1]
    			t2.animator.fire_multiplier = if v3[6] then v1:read_u8() else 0 / 64
    			t2.animator.parallel_barrel_look_buffer.use_velocity = not v3[3]
    			local v17 = t2.animator:set_nvd(v4)
    			t2.animator:set_aiming(v3[2])
    			local v18 = SharedTable.new()
    			v18.accessories_state = {
    				flashlight_enabled = v3[5],
    				laser_enabled = v3[4],
    			}
    			if v3[7] then
    				local v20 = NetworkEncode.read_position(v1)
    				t.velocity = NetworkEncode.read_velocity(v1)
    				t2.animator.parallel_position_buffer:push_entry({
    				})
    			if v3[8] then
    				t2.animator:set_lean(NetworkEncode.read_lean(v1))
    			if v3[9] then
    				local v21 = NetworkEncode.read_look(v1)
    				t2.animator.parallel_look_buffer:push_entry({
    				})
    					v18.look_activity = (v21 - v2).Magnitude
    			if v3[10] then
    				t2.animator.parallel_barrel_look_buffer:push_entry({
    					position = NetworkEncode.read_look(v1),
    				})
    			if v3[11] then
    				local v222 = NetworkEncode.read_pose(v1)
    				t2.animator:set_pose(v222)
    				send_bindable_message(v8, {
    				})
    				send_bindable_message(v8, v18)
    				send_bindable_message(v8, {
    				})
    	end))
    	v32:GiveTask(RunService.RenderStepped:ConnectParallel(function(p1) --[[ Line: 225 | Upvalues: v12 (ref), v62 (copy) ]]
    			v62:client_step(p1)
    	end))
    	v32:GiveTask(RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(p1) --[[ Line: 231 | Upvalues: v12 (ref), v62 (copy) ]]
    			v62:position_update(p1)
    	end))
    	v32:GiveTask(v6:Connect(function(p1, p2, p3) --[[ Line: 238 | Upvalues: ingame_id (copy), v5 (copy), send_bindable_message (ref), v8 (ref), character (copy), v12 (ref), v62 (copy), quality (copy), v32 (copy), v4 (copy) ]]
    			v5:trace("character died, marking as dead")
    			send_bindable_message(v8, {
    			})
    			send_bindable_message(v8, {
    			})
    			v62:limb_update(false)
    			v62:do_ragdoll(p2 * quality.ragdoll_strength, p3)
    			v32:DoCleaning()
    			task.delay(1, function() --[[ Line: 257 | Upvalues: v4 (ref) ]]
    				return v4:DoCleaning()
    			end)
    	end))
    	v5:trace("sending msgback")
    	send_bindable_message(v8, {
    	})
